Franco-Italian Agreement Unfolds 20

Encompassing Politics, Military Affairs, and Economics

France Underwrites Italian Securities Worth Two Million

Rome Today, it was learned that the political and military agreement between Italy and France has expanded its scope to include economic and financial issues. Therefore, the two countries have practically combined to become a kind of Central European peaceful dictatorship. The National Bank of France has agreed to underwrite Italian securities worth two million lire. This agreement, which can be signed in Geneva soon, will completely change the lines of European powers after the combination of Italy and France. The ideal theory of disarmament will be replaced by a realized system of peaceful dictatorship. It is said that the Franco-Italian agreement will not have many problems with the Little Entente countries. The diplomatic community believes that the Danube River countries will therefore broaden their horizons, and the result will make it easier for them to realize their wishes. The points currently stipulated in the Franco-Italian agreement are as follows: (1) Naval equality; (2) Armed forces equality; (3) Jointly refuse German rearmament; and (4) Implement political cooperation on international affairs. Italian and French politicians all expect that the Little Entente countries will eventually join. If so, the resolutions of the countries participating in the agreement will have the backing of 1.5 million standing troops. The beginning of the combination of Italy and France was due to Germany's recent actions in Austria and the failure of the disarmament conference. (30th Dispatch from the Kuomin)

Austrian Rumors Flare Up Again 21

Saying that the Home Guard is Dissatisfied with the Status Quo and Plots Rebellion

Vienna Today, rumors are rife, saying that the Home Guard is planning to revolt because they are dissatisfied with their current position and fear that they will be disbanded. The Home Guard is a semi-military organization, very similar to the German National Socialist Party and the Italian Blackshirts. It was established several years ago, and its leader is the current Deputy Prime Minister Prince Starhemberg. After being recognized by the government, it became an auxiliary police organization. It made great contributions to the government during the Social Democratic Party uprising in February and the National Socialist Party rebellion in July. (30th Dispatch from Reuters)

Vienna When Austrian former Prime Minister Seipel was in office, he was assassinated by thugs, and his physical strength declined. He passed away several years ago. Former Prime Minister Dollfuss was also murdered by the National Socialist Party this year. The Austrian party authorities, remembering that Seipel and Dollfuss had devoted themselves to the country and sacrificed themselves for Austrian independence, held a memorial ceremony for the two former prime ministers today. The memorial service was held in St. Stephen's Cathedral. President Miklas, Prime Minister Schuschnigg, other government ministers, and the diplomatic corps all attended in person. After the memorial service, the coffins of the two former prime ministers were placed in a hearse pulled by eight black horses, led by the Presidential Guard cavalry, and transported to the Seipel and Dollfuss church for burial. When the coffins were displayed in the cathedral, many people went to pay their respects. (29th Dispatch from Havas)

Spain

Cabinet Fate Uncertain 23

Parliament May Be Dissolved

Madrid The Spanish political situation is repeating the cycle of events. The history of a year ago is now being repeated. It is still remembered that when the House of Representatives adjourned at the end of September 1933 and held a meeting, the Lerroux cabinet began to embark on the path of reliance. At that time, the theory of dissolving the House of Representatives was all the rage. Now, at the end of September 1934, the political situation is exactly the same as it was a year ago. The Samper cabinet has only been established for five months, and its fate is already precarious due to the reopening of the House of Representatives. Newspapers are also spreading rumors of dissolving the House of Representatives. As for whether the current cabinet is about to collapse, observers often hold different opinions. Some people have always doubted the cabinet's overthrow, believing that the current cabinet can pass the budget bill through the House of Representatives. However, there are very few people who make this kind of speculation. Llopis, the leader of the Acción Popular party, which advocates Pan-Hispanism, clearly announced in Catalonia that the party had decided to stop supporting the current government and was prepared to directly participate in the government. Llopis's opinion has not changed so far. As for the Agrarian Party and the Monarchist Party, they are even more dissatisfied with the Samper cabinet due to the Catalonian land issue. Judging from this, when the House of Representatives meets tomorrow, the cabinet can only rely on the eighty votes of the Radical Party and some other independent members. The Spanish House of Representatives has a total of 459 members, so it is very difficult to obtain a majority. Unless new facts occur (such as those related to public order), the development of the political tide seems to be predictable. As for the proposal to dissolve the House of Representatives, it is mostly seen in the left-wing newspapers. The right-wing believes that this is a movement to oppose the constitutional procedure for resolving the cabinet tide. In short, if the cabinet is overthrown, it will be very difficult to resolve the political tide. Unless Lerroux, the former Prime Minister of the Radical Party, resumes his post as Prime Minister, any new cabinet does not seem to be able to obtain the support of the Radical Party. However, it is rumored by the government that President Zamora's friendship with Lerroux has greatly diminished due to various facts before the cabinet tide occurred in April of this year. In this case, it is very unlikely that Lerroux will form a cabinet. In addition, some people said that Llopis of the right-wing Acción Popular party requested to select four seats in the cabinet and give them to his political friends. Although the Acción Popular party, which has extreme right-wing tendencies, has repeatedly announced that it is willing to accept the political system chosen by public opinion, it has never been heard that the party members clearly announced that they are republicans. In this case, can President Zamora tolerate the placement of such people in the cabinet's internal affairs, army, and agriculture departments? And if Llopis's faction joins the new cabinet, the left-wing and socialist congressmen will vote against it. It can be further asserted that if President Zamora considers this, it is a big question whether he can accept Llopis's request. Although the answers to various questions cannot be given at present, if the cabinet tide cannot be resolved, then it is difficult to avoid another dissolution of the Spanish parliament. (30th Dispatch from Havas)

Lindbergh Kidnapping Case

Continued Arrests 25

Strange Woman Testifies in Court

(New York) Bronx District Attorney Foley announced today that Hauptmann, the suspect in the Lindbergh baby kidnapping and murder case, has been charged with receiving $50,000 in ransom and will be formally tried on October 10. Foley said that the jurors will probably be local gentlemen. The police department stated that the crime of receiving ransom has been conclusively proven, but the murder charge has not yet been filed. It is also heard that the authorities are preparing to interrogate a woman named Mary, because she talked about the Lindbergh kidnapping case for hours before the reason for Hauptmann's arrest was announced. The authorities are also paying close attention to Bowman, a suspect arrested in Chicago yesterday, but they are unwilling to express their opinions. (29th Dispatch from the Kuomin)

Chicago As a result of the search by New York detectives, two more people were arrested today. It is heard that Bowman, who is related to the Lindbergh baby kidnapping case, is believed by the police to be the person who has been wanted for a long time and who received $50,000 in ransom from Dr. Condon under the alias John. The other person is a woman named Felice, who initially claimed to be Bowman's mistress and then denied it. (29th Dispatch from Reuters)

(New York) Judicial authorities continue to investigate the Lindbergh baby kidnapping case. Today, a strange woman testified in court. The interrogation was extremely secretive. This woman seemed to have extremely important testimony, but the inspectors believed that the evidence presented by this woman only affected one person, namely, Hauptmann. Two doctors specializing in nervous diseases have examined Hauptmann, one of whom was hired by the defendant, and both are unwilling to express their opinions. (29th Dispatch from Havas)

In France, there is a person named Ulrik in the port of Cherbourg who is suspected of being involved in the kidnapping case of U.S. Colonel Lindbergh's beloved son, but has not been arrested. Australian Female Aviator

Flies Solo to Australia 27

Has Now Arrived Safely in Marseille

(London) Australian female aviator Thomson set off from Lympne airfield yesterday in a Moth aircraft, attempting to complete the feat of being the first Australian female aviator to fly solo from England to Australia. Although the weather was bad on the first leg of the journey, the lady's progress was quite smooth. Since departing from England, there has been no news, and the general public has been quite worried. However, Ms. Thomson finally arrived safely in Marseille at 11:52 this morning. It is heard that the reason for the delay was that the weather was bad en route, and she was forced to land in Nîmes. In order to make up for the delay, Ms. Thomson took off for Rome after refueling and arrived safely in the Italian capital in the afternoon. (29th Dispatch from Reuters)

Napoleon's Collection of Books 29

Donated to Princeton University

Princeton, New Jersey, U.S. Banker Taylor donated part of Napoleon I's collection of books to Princeton University today. According to reports, in 1815, Napoleon was defeated and exiled to Saint Helena Island. His collection of books was seized by the British-Prussian Allied Forces and then sold to Queen Marie Louise during the Paris Peace Conference. Later, it was lost, and its whereabouts were unknown for a hundred years. It only appeared in Germany a few years ago. Part of it fell into Taylor's hands, and the rest was preserved by the French government. (20th Dispatch from Havas)

German Oil Well Catches Fire 31

(Berlin) The Ninshagen oil well in Hanover, the largest oil well in Germany, suddenly caught fire this morning. It has been burning since 7:00 AM, and four workers are missing. Another eleven were seriously injured. It is feared that the missing have been buried in the fire. According to reports, the well was dug seven months ago and is 3,000 feet deep. The disaster this morning was caused by a strong outburst of gas in the well catching fire. (29th Dispatch from Reuters)

Labor Minister Discusses

Labor Relief Measures 33

University Students Get Close to Workers

Farmers Get Close to City Dwellers

(National News Agency, Berlin Special Dispatch, September 23rd) The German unemployment problem has been effectively relieved through measures taken by the Ministry of Labor. A reporter interviewed Labor Minister Scheldt about labor relief measures. According to his discussion, all human systems have been in constant change for nearly a century. Therefore, amidst this global unemployment crisis, we must find ways to provide relief. The causes of unemployment are numerous and varied, with some being common to all countries and others being unique. Some may be due to the special circumstances of a particular country, leading to unemployment panic. However, the root cause of unemployment is not the most important thing; rather, we must observe the facts and seek solutions and ways out with a clear vision. How can we provide relief and eliminate the source of the disaster?

In Germany (or perhaps not only Germany), as in other countries, there is ongoing discussion of comprehensive methods to prevent youth unemployment and restore customs, order, and social peace after the end of the Great War. Everyone is linked to the nation, and everyone has patriotic ideas, which gives the German government a strong backing in this situation. Currently, there are a total of 250,000 workers in Germany, who are working together to create wealth for the country. Everyone has a fundamental idea of promoting industry, which is very beneficial to the national economy and order. From a humanitarian point of view, let's briefly discuss this. We must properly arrange everything. We must improve the lives of workers so that all workers do not perish and die. Rescue the youth, but the people of the country are not very clear about this, only knowing that this matter is terrible. Recently, the Implementation Committee of the Geneva Disarmament Conference has discussed the issue of labor relief, using formal methods to rescue German youth. Because the important issue of labor relief starts with education and personality, and social conditions must be paid attention to first. We should not only discuss it in terms of Germany, but should extend it to all countries, and France must not misunderstand it. The German government has no despicable views, and does not use labor relief to seek to enrich military equipment. If you do not believe it, you can go to Germany to see and know that Germany is dedicated to solving the difficulties of the labor sector, and there are no other military purposes, it is for the workers to serve. Therefore, labor relief is not malicious, but to save unemployed youth, so that the German people will not be in chaos in the future.

If we want to talk about relieving labor in Germany, we must first seek good methods, which must be suitable for the character of German youth and the entire German national character. The best thing we can do is to refer to the past experience of various countries, such as referring to the methods of Bulgaria, because their country is also in difficulty, rescuing all labor circles. If we can participate in the labor relief methods of various countries to relieve the unemployed people in Germany, then in the future German youth will have a ray of hope. Now no one in the world can realize this hope with the methods of human ethics and justice. In this difficulty, people of all classes should discuss ways together, take joint responsibility, cooperate and serve the people, and lead young people into the norms of righteousness and etiquette. All university students should also approach manual workers and workers, farmers should approach city dwellers, the learned should approach the unlearned, and the ignorant should be created to serve others. Everyone should do their best, provide free relief, avoid class conflicts, and avoid the death of people. Under the leadership of Hitler, eliminate class struggles, because society is different, it is appropriate to jointly relieve unemployment, and surpassing the contradictory thinking of class struggles is the supreme method. All people created by God should coexist and prosper.

If our main goal is to relieve the good order and education of the labor sector, if so, there should be no risk of failure. The national economy is what we should strive for, and the focus is on relieving labor, so it does not compete with the individual economy. The situation in various countries today is very clear. There can be no good results and methods on the path of a free individual economy, nor can the problem of the national economy be solved. The individual economy cannot relieve the unemployment problem, or completely solve the unemployment problem, it only belongs to the private ownership of entrepreneurs. For example, opening up wasteland, irrigating fields, such as opening up roads and other enterprises, is beneficial to the public and everyone can take it and use it unconditionally. However, in the autumn of crisis and survival, the individual economy should not be put in a dangerous situation, and we should not despise it. The individual economy has its own meaning for the country. When the country changes from a non-terrorist state to a terrorist state, or when it is reorganizing streets and facilitating traffic, when the highway is not developed, the individual economy can build everything for the country. Labor relief can be freely worked according to the rules, and the strength of thousands of people must be gathered to work together. Under this situation, it is appropriate to solve or use unused labor force directly in the aspect of free relief, use production methods to sell surplus goods, and the individual economy is the first to start labor undertakings, and always help people have the opportunity to obtain work, but sometimes the individual economy also publicly destroys labor undertakings, and various countries and government agencies pay close attention to this, because the individual economy cannot directly have the ability to produce. Now is not the time for the country to take this opportunity to implement a large economic plan. If the country wants to encourage public enterprises at present, it cannot be delayed. The government of the German Republic is implementing this principle wholeheartedly. Everyone can freely relieve labor, and the results will be considerable. I guarantee in the name of the Minister of Labor that our leader Hitler will be able to bravely implement the cause of labor relief.

New Soviet Machine Factory Opens 37

(Moscow) The Stalin Machine Manufacturing Plant, newly built in Kramatorsk, Donetsk Region, has opened. All Soviet newspapers reported it with significant coverage. The factory will start operating in the coming days, producing six blast furnaces, thirty open-hearth furnaces, three cast iron furnaces, sixteen rolling mills, and heavy cranes, machinery for the chemical and coking industries, diesel engines, boilers, and internal combustion engines. Pravda said that the opening of the Kramatorsk plant has made the Soviet Union the most advanced country in the world in the production of heavy machinery. The factory is a commemorative expression of the Soviet era of industrialization, and is therefore a symbol of the maturity of Soviet industry and its invincible national defense capabilities. (29th TASS Dispatch)

British Dominion Bond Regulations 38

Regulations for the issuance of Ottawa Dominion refunding bonds were announced today, amounting to $250 million. The two-year bonds realized 98.90, with interest at 2.57 percent. The five-year bonds realized 98.15, with interest at 2.9 percent. The eight-year bonds realized 97, with interest at 3.47 percent. The fifteen-year bonds realized 96.5, with interest at 3.81 percent. The funds raised, totaling $222 million, will be used to repay the 5 percent interest Victory Bonds due on November 1st. Holders of Victory Bonds who wish to exchange them for eight-year or fifteen-year new bonds will receive special treatment. The new bonds will open on October 1st and close on the 13th. (29th Reuters Dispatch)

The War Zone Readjustment Committee Will Be Established in Advance 80

Participants Largely Designated

Japanese Planes Scatter Leaflets Again

(North China Dispatch) The Political Readjustment Committee recently decided to organize a War Zone Readjustment Committee, with seven organizations as constituent members, including the Military Sub-Committee, the Hebei and Chahar Provincial Governments, the Beining Railway Bureau, and the special offices of the Jizhou-Miyun and Luan-Yu Districts. Due to the complexity of issues in the war zone that urgently need resolution, Huang Fu has sent letters to relevant organizations designating participants. In addition to the representatives of the Military Sub-Committee, Zhu Shiqin; the Political Readjustment Committee, Li Zeyi; the Beining Railway Bureau, Yin Tong; and the two special offices, Yin Rugeng and Tao Shangming, the Chahar Provincial Government is expected to appoint the foreign affairs commissioner Yue Kaixian, and the Hebei Provincial Government is expected to appoint Zhang Houwan. Regarding the organizational rules of the committee, Huang Fu convened Tao Shangming, Yin Rugeng, Yin Tong, and Li Zeyi yesterday morning to begin discussions, which will continue at 10 a.m. today (the 29th). Li Zeyi will be responsible for convening the participants to complete the discussions within a limited time. If the rules can be finalized before the 30th, the committee can be established in advance to begin addressing the issues in the war zone. In the counties of Yutian and Zunhua within the jurisdiction of the Jizhou-Miyun District, bandits have emerged since the 23rd, occupying places like Xiaolizhuang, Huangjiashan, Matoushan, and Letaicun in Yutian, engaging in extensive burning and looting. Wang Zhanyuan, the captain of the 3rd Brigade of the War Zone Security Team, dispatched troops to suppress the bandits in different directions. After encountering the bandits, some of them fled to Qiujiatun and outside the Jieshankou area, resisting the pursuing security team and local militia with the terrain. At dawn today (the 29th), the security team was ordered to search for the bandits, but they had all fled without a trace. Captain Wu Zhanyuan and Yutian County Magistrate Chen Baosheng reported this to Yin Rugeng and Wei Yonghe via telegram today (the 29th) and are making efforts to investigate the losses in the affected villages, as well as dispatching teams to continue searching for remaining bandits.

Since the signing of the Tanggu Truce, Japanese planes had not been scattering leaflets for a long time, but from the 27th of this month, Japanese planes have been flying from Rehe via Gubeikou to Miyun, Jixian, Sanhe, Zunhua, and other places from time to time, dropping leaflets. The leaflets dropped in Gubeikou were printed in red and green newspaper ink, with very simple sentences expressing that the responsibility for the Yutian Miyakoshi case should be pursued. (29th)

Japan

Combined Fleet Arrives in Qingdao 81

Total of Sixty-Eight Warships

Forty-Five Thousand Officers and Men

Suetsugu Will Proceed to Jinan from Qingdao

(Qingdao Dispatch) The First and Second Combined Fleets of Japan, totaling sixty-eight warships, are the most powerful main fleet of the Japanese Navy. The flagship is the Kongo, with a displacement of over 29,000 tons, and the total number of officers and men is 45,000. This morning (the 28th) at 11:00 a.m., led by Commander-in-Chief Admiral Suetsugu, the fleet arrived in Qingdao from Japan for a visit. The ships entered the harbor one after another and berthed in the front and rear bays. All staff members of the Japanese Consulate in Qingdao, as well as Japanese residents, went to the pier to welcome them. Mr. Suetsugu went ashore from the front bay pier at 12:00 noon and took a car to the city government to pay respects to Mayor Shen Honglie. At 3:00 p.m., Shen visited the ship in return. At 6:00 p.m. that evening, Japanese Consul-General Sakane and Japanese residents held a banquet for all officers of the fleet at the Japanese Residents' Association, inviting Mayor Shen, City Government Secretary-General Hu Jiafeng, Councilors Zhou Jiayan, Yang Jinsheng, and heads of various bureaus as guests. Japanese residents have also scheduled a grand welcoming party at the Japanese Residents' Association at noon on the 29th. In order to foster closer ties, Mayor Shen has scheduled a banquet at the Yingbin Hotel on the evening of the 30th for the main officers of the fleet, and all officers of the rank of Colonel and above have been invited. Mr. Suetsugu is scheduled to lead some officers to Jinan on the 29th to inspect battlefields, and will return to Qingdao on the 30th. The remaining officers and men are scheduled to go ashore on the 29th to pay respects at the Loyalty Monument and the Japanese Shrine, and to visit the German Fort and the Japanese-German battlefields. Mr. Suetsugu is scheduled to host a banquet on the Kongo at 2:00 p.m. on October 1st to entertain Chinese and Japanese officials, and will leave Qingdao for other destinations on the 2nd. The names of all ships are listed as follows: Battleships Kongo, Fuso, Hyuga, Kirishima; Cruisers Takao, Maya; Aircraft Carrier Akagi; Cruisers Aoba, Kinugasa, Furutaka, Kako, Naka, Yura, Natori; Transport Ship Kamui; Submarine Tender Jingei; 6th Destroyer Division Hibiki, Ikazuchi; Aircraft Carrier Ryujo; Cruiser Isuzu; 12th Destroyer Division Shirakumo, Murakumo, Shinonome; Cruiser Nagara; 23rd Destroyer Division Kikutsuki, Minatsuki, Mochizuki, Satsuki; Submarine Tender Chogei; 10th Destroyer Division Akatsuki, Sagiri, Sazanami; Transport Ship Naruto; Cruiser Sendai; 11th Destroyer Division Hatsuyuki, Shirayuki; Transport Ship Tsurumi; 5th Destroyer Division Matsukaze, Harukaze, Hatakaze, Asakaze; 29th Destroyer Division Hayate, Oite, Yufure, Asanagi; Transport Ship Mamiya; 8th Submarine I-5, I-4; 30th Destroyer Division Mutzuki, Utsuki, Kisaragi, Yayoi; 7th Submarine Division I-1, I-2, I-3; 19th Submarine Division I-58, I-57, I-56; 2nd Destroyer Division Kamikaze, Nadakaze, Yakaze; 29th Submarine Division I-64, I-61, I-62; 30th Submarine Division I-66, I-67, I-65.

(Jinan Dispatch) Admiral Suetsugu Nobumasa, commander of the Japanese Combined Fleet, leading the entire fleet of warships and 45,000 officers and soldiers, arrived in Qingdao on the afternoon of the 28th. At 10 p.m. that night, he, along with Vice Admiral Takahashi and eight other attendants, as well as the military attache Hanatani who welcomed him in Qingdao, boarded the Jiaoji Railway train to the west. This morning (the 29th) at 7:15 a.m., they arrived in Jinan. The Japanese consul in Jinan, Nishida, and hundreds of Japanese residents, each holding a national flag, welcomed them at the station and took a group photo. Suetsugu also inspected the construction project of the building under construction at the Jiaoji Railway Station, and then took a car directly to the Japanese Consulate to rest. At 9:30 a.m., he, along with Nishida and Hanatani, paid a visit to Han Fuju, chairman of the provincial government. Han hosted a banquet. After leaving, at noon, he attended a public banquet hosted by the Japanese residents in Jinan. Suetsugu is scheduled to take the Jiaoji Railway train back to Qingdao at 10 p.m. tonight. A reporter interviewed Suetsugu at the Japanese Consulate today. Suetsugu made the following brief remarks: "Our fleet has been to Dalian ('Manchukuo'), Lushun, Yantai, and other places. Yesterday we arrived in Qingdao. There is no special mission for this trip to Jinan. Because there are many Japanese residents in Jiaodong, I came to take a look. I have not been to China for long, so I have no special feelings. However, I heard that things in Shandong are going very well. In short, it is very important that China and Japan should be on good terms, not just on the surface, but truly good, and that the two countries should unite to protect the peace and security of the East. At 9:30 a.m. today, I visited Chairman Han and plan to return to Qingdao at 10 p.m. tonight. I plan to stay in Qingdao for two or three days to exchange greetings with local officials and visit various places. After finishing in Qingdao, I will not go anywhere else and will return home directly," and so on. (29th)

Northern Sichuan Refugees Awaiting Relief 82

Liu Xiang Telephones Central Government Requesting Funds

(Chongqing Dispatch) Recently, refugees from Tongnan and Banan have been moving and fleeing, visible along the banks of the Jialing River. Supporting the old and carrying the young, they lack even thin porridge. The situation is extremely dire. Although the headquarters has telegraphed various counties in northern Sichuan to set up shelters and expedite emergency relief, the number of refugees is too large and the relief is insufficient. The disaster victims are crying out for food, barely surviving, and the situation is extremely urgent. Liu Xiang telegraphed the Central Government yesterday, imploring the Ministry of Finance to quickly allocate large sums of money to address the immediate crisis. At the same time, Tian Songyao also sent a telegram to the headquarters, asking Liu to forward it to the Central Government. Both are recorded below:

(1) (Respectfully addressed to Lin, Chairman of the National Government of Nanjing; Wang, President of the Executive Yuan; and Jiang, Chairman of the Nanchang Military Affairs Commission: I have carefully investigated that the Red bandits have caused devastation in Sichuan. In the past, I received 300,000 yuan for disaster relief, which was allocated to various disaster areas. The care and kindness are deeply appreciated. Recently, reports from various sources have stated that the refugees are displaced and in a dire state. I implore you to find ways to provide relief. My efforts have been insufficient, and I am deeply ashamed. I have exhausted my resources and cannot provide further support. I have ordered my subordinates to provide shelter, but our strength is limited. I know that you are deeply concerned about the suffering and take responsibility for the hungry and drowning. Think of the refugees exposed to the elements, awaiting relief, their hopes as high as the clouds, their survival uncertain from morning to evening. Moreover, with the Red bandits rampant, the rear is critical. Driven by hunger and cold, I fear that the able-bodied will become bandits, which is pitiful. Lamenting the old and weak dying in ditches, without immediate and extensive assistance, it will be impossible to avert this catastrophe. I implore you to order the Ministry of Finance to quickly allocate large sums of money to Sichuan for disaster relief, so as to prevent displacement. Then the people of Sichuan will be grateful for your kindness and benevolence. In addition to sending separate telegrams, I respectfully submit this telegram, awaiting your orders with utmost apprehension. Respectfully, Liu Xiang.)

(2) (Respectfully addressed to Lin, Chairman of the National Government; and Wang, President of the Executive Yuan: I have received the telegram from Tian Songyao (code seventeen), commander of the 29th Army, stating that refugees from Tongnan and Ba counties fleeing from the bandits have crossed the Jialing River, increasing tenfold compared to before. They are displaced and in an extremely miserable state. In addition to ordering the counties in the military districts to provide shelter and relief, the number of refugees is too large, making comprehensive assistance extremely difficult. I request that you find ways to raise funds for relief and forward this to the Central Government to allocate large sums of money for assistance. I have investigated that with the shift in the front lines of bandit suppression in northern Sichuan, the number of refugees has increased, and they are suffering greatly. Providing relief requires large sums of money. The drought and flood disasters in various counties of this province are extremely severe, making it difficult to raise funds locally. I implore you to consider the plight of the refugees and quickly order the Ministry of Finance to allocate large sums of money for relief to benefit the disaster victims. I am urgently awaiting your orders. Respectfully, Liu Xiang, Commander-in-Chief of Sichuan Bandit Suppression, with Guo Changming, Chief of Staff, acting on his behalf.)

Fourth Sheet 83

Fujian Border Bandit Suppression Triumphant News 84

Rapid Progress of National Army Along Xingguo-Shicheng-Changting Line

Commander of Pseudo-Third Army Corps Zhang Yi Surrenders

(Nanchang Dispatch) Since the bandits were repeatedly surrounded and suppressed by the National Army, their elite forces have been almost entirely lost. The newly recruited bandit soldiers are purely a motley crowd, unable to withstand a single blow from the National Army. Currently, the bandits' combat troops, nominally numbering more than ten divisions, are distributed in three directions: Xingguo, Shicheng, and Changting, attempting to defend the bandit areas in order to prolong their existence. On the 22nd, the National Army's Zhou Column had already captured the line of Lantianxu and Xintian. In this battle, the Pseudo-First Army Corps' Second Division and the Pseudo-Fifth Army Corps' Thirteenth and Thirty-Fourth Divisions suffered more than 2,000 casualties and fled in disarray towards the vicinity of Gaoxingxu. The National Army is still tracking and suppressing them, and Xingguo is only thirty li away, and it will not be difficult to take it in one go. In the Shicheng area, the National Army's Third Route Army also captured Zhongzizhai, Zhonghuashan, Chenguling, Fenshuijun, and other places on the 26th and 27th. The bandits resisting the National Army were the Pseudo-Third Army Corps' Fourth and Fifth Divisions, and the Pseudo-First Army Corps' Fifteenth Division. The battle was fierce, and the bandits' casualties were estimated to be over 3,000. The commander of the Pseudo-Third Army Corps' Fourth Division, Zhang Yi, also became enlightened and led his troops to surrender. He stated that the strength of the bandit army has suffered several losses, and even if they wanted to replenish it, it would be impossible, because the able-bodied men in the bandit areas have already been exhausted. The bandit soldiers are all in a state of panic, and the people are also complaining. Moreover, there is discrimination and mutual sabotage within the bandits, and the time of their disintegration is not far away. Shicheng is now under the control of the National Army's artillery and air power, and recovery is imminent. Currently, in the Changting area, there are only the Pseudo-Ninth Army Corps' Third Division and the Pseudo-Twenty-Fourth Division, with fewer than 3,000 bandits. The National Army's Eastern Route is advancing towards Changting from Pengkou and captured the bandits' most fortified position, Baiyi Yangling, on the 27th of this month. The bandits suffered more than 1,000 casualties, and the attack is continuing. It will only take a few days to reach Changting.

A Northwest Inspection Report: Our Special Correspondent, Geng Ya 85

Overview of Xining and the Scenery of Qinghai

Xining is located on the shaded side of the Xiaojishi Mountain and is the leading district of Qinghai. The climate is relatively cold, with summer temperatures only reaching 80 degrees Fahrenheit and winter temperatures dropping below zero. The Huangshui River traverses the area, and its downstream can be used for rafting. The land is fertile, and the production is particularly abundant. According to a survey, the county has 21,754.93 mu of arable land, 241,515.37 mu of barren land, totaling 263,170.3 mu. In 1929, Gansu experienced a severe drought, and Lanzhou's food supply depended entirely on shipments from here. In recent years, grain prices have also been lower than elsewhere. It is a pity that grain merchants only transport goods with livestock, which is inconvenient. The county has a population of approximately 170,000, with Han Chinese accounting for 64%, Hui Muslims for 20%, and the Tu and Tibetan groups each accounting for 8%. In the past, Hui-Han relations were prone to rifts, but recently, due to the authorities in government and the military not discriminating and working together, the people are gradually becoming more harmonious. The Tu and Tibetan groups have limited knowledge and have long been assimilated by the Han Chinese.

The city borders the southern bank of the Huangshui River, surrounded by mountains and ridges, with a magnificent landscape. It is the first of the four major trading areas for Han and Tibetan peoples and the eastern gateway to Qinghai. In 1928, Qinghai was established as a province, and it was designated as the provincial capital. Government agencies were set up, and the number of schools increased. Currently, there are seven secondary schools: the Mongolian-Tibetan Normal School, the Provincial First High School, the First Normal School, the Girls' Normal School, the Agricultural School, the Vocational School, and the Hui Islamic Advancement Association Middle School (the Hui Islamic Advancement Association High School and the Xining Branch of the Central Political School, which includes Mongolian and Tibetan studies, are also about to open). These schools have approximately 2,100 students. There are many elementary schools, with more than 3,000 students. Other counties only have a junior high school in Ledu, and the rest are only elementary schools. Funding is difficult, making it difficult to promote education. The students' lives are also very difficult, but their bodies are quite healthy. The Hui Islamic Advancement Association Middle School and the elementary schools run by the county branches have sufficient funding and are thriving.

Wang Qian, the chief of the military law department, and Zhu Guangtian, the director, of the 100th Division Headquarters, successively hosted dinners and introduced friends familiar with the situation in Qinghai, which was very beneficial. According to Qiu Xianglu, the secretary-general of the Provincial Party Headquarters, there are more than 490 party members in Qinghai Province, with formal and probationary members accounting for half each. The county party headquarters have canceled the former workers' and peasants' associations and other groups because they could not seek the interests of the people and became fundraising organizations that exploited the people. They are focusing on promoting social education, such as establishing libraries and creating literacy schools. The province currently has publications, the most prominent of which is the Republican Daily, founded on July 1, 1929. At that time, the National Revolutionary Army occupied the Northwest, and news from other provinces was isolated. The printing was poor, and the content was simple. In 1931, the Special Commissioner's Office of the Provincial Party Affairs Department was established, and a radio room was set up. News broadcast by the Central Broadcasting Station every day was transcribed and published, and the content gradually became more substantial. In June 1933, a hand-cranked printing machine donated by the Central Government was received, and copper printing was adopted. However, due to the narrow administrative scope of the province, it was difficult to collect news, and funding was difficult, so only one sheet of quarto paper was published each day. Plans for expansion are currently underway. In addition, there is the Qinghai Review bi-monthly, which is sponsored by the Provincial Party Special Office; the 100th Weekly, which is sponsored by the Special Party Headquarters of the 100th Division; the To the People Weekly, which is sponsored by Song Shouyi, the rural instructor of the Provincial Party Special Office. Huzhu, Datong, and Huangyuan counties each publish a weekly newspaper by their respective county party headquarters. Each newspaper is printed in 200-300 copies and is mostly distributed as gifts. In addition, Ma Yusan, the president of the local court, is also planning to establish a National Daily.

Li Xiaozhong, the secretary-general of the Special Party Headquarters of the 100th Division, said that the division has participated in many battles, roughly as follows: In March 1928, Ma Zhongying incited a rebellion in Dahe, and the National Revolutionary Army's suppression was ineffective. Division Commander Ma Bufang, who was then the commander of the 77th Brigade, participated in the war in March 1929, cleared the remaining bandits, and pacified Dahe. In July 1930, Ma Tingxian incited a rebellion in Longnan. At that time, Division Commander Ma was the commander of the Provisional First Division of Qinghai. Wang Zhen, the acting chairman of Gansu, telegraphed requesting the dispatch of troops for joint suppression and recovered Dingxi County. In the autumn of 1930, Ma Zhongying led his remnant troops to occupy the area of Ganliang, arbitrarily persecuting the people. Division Commander Ma was then the commander of the newly formed Ninth Division and moved to Zhangye and Jiuquan counties according to the telegram from Chairman Gu Zhutong of Tongguan. Ma Zhongying retreated into Xinjiang, and Hexi was pacified. In July 1931, Lei Zhongtian, commander of the newly formed Eighth Division of Gansu, violated the Central Government and detained Chairman Ma Hongbin. Division Commander Ma advised him to be prudent and resolve the issue. In April 1932, Tibetan soldiers, instigated by British imperialists, invaded Hainan, occupied Dasuomang, Nangqian, and other places, and besieged Jiegu. The Qinghai provincial government was reluctant to engage in fratricidal conflict and first sent envoy Ma Xun to persuade the troops to withdraw, but it was ineffective. Later, troops were dispatched to support and recover the lost territory, and both sides sent personnel to negotiate peace. In the summer of 1933, the Central Government appointed Sun Dianying as the Qinghai Reclamation Commissioner. Subsequently, the Central Government, considering the opinions of the people of Gansu, Ningxia, and Qinghai, telegraphed Sun to postpone his westward advance. Sun took advantage of the outbreak of the Fujian Incident and occupied Dengkou in January of this year and besieged Ningxia. Division Commander Ma received a telegram from Director Zhu Shaoliang ordering him to send troops to Ningxia and cooperate with the 35th Division of the 15th Route Army to fight against the old rebels. The enemy completely retreated on the night of March 18, and the Ningxia area was preserved. Although this is the history of struggle of only one division in a few short years, it also reflects one page of the recent frequent changes experienced by the people of Gansu, Ningxia, and Qinghai, who are like brothers in distress.

Upstream of the Huanghe River is a large lake called Qinghai, from which the province gets its name. It is 270 li from Xining to the sea, which can be reached in three days on horseback. In summer and autumn, it appears as a vast expanse of blue, as if floating in the sky and about to pour down. The terrain is very high, about 7,100 feet above sea level. The perimeter of the sea is not yet accurately known. Some say it is 600 li, others say it is 800 li. The Tibetans say that it takes 18 days to ride a horse around the sea, which would be at least 1,000 li. The water is extremely clear, contains salt, and tastes salty and delicious. It is rumored to be a weak water that cannot float mustard seeds, but this is not true. However, the wind and waves are extremely large and continuous throughout the year. Aquatic birds and grass leaves are washed to the edge by the waves. Not only is it extremely difficult to sail ships, but the surrounding wilderness within a hundred li cannot be cultivated due to the strong winds. The sea is rich in fish, without scales, with black spots on the back, called Huang fish. In summer, the Tibetans strike them with sticks, and in winter, they catch them by drilling holes. The abdomen is cut open, the intestines are removed, and they are dried on the spot. The ground contains salt, which prevents them from rotting. However, the Tibetans have other concerns (the reasons are detailed elsewhere) and do not eat fish, so they are mostly transported to other counties for sale, amounting to hundreds of thousands of jin per year. There are two mountains in the sea, one resembling a snail shell and the other resembling a camel hump, located in the east and west, called Haixin Mountain. Temples are built on them, with dozens of lamas. In winter, when the sea is frozen, they drive cattle and horses, transporting fur to various counties in Huangyuan in exchange for food to prepare for the whole year. Southwest of the sea is a salt pond, which is very rich in production, of good quality and delicious taste, forming square crystals. Fifty li east of the sea is the Sea God Temple. Every autumn, the Qinghai authorities send letters to summon Mongolian princes to hold a grand alliance ceremony here. The ceremony is simple but contains significant political significance.

In the summer of 1907 (Gregorian calendar), the Russian Kozlov crossed Qinghai in a cloth boat to Haixin Mountain. When the Mongolians and Tibetans saw him, they were amazed and thought he was a celestial being. Kozlov discovered that Haixin Mountain is located in the middle of the lake and its geology is composed of granite and mica schist. The deepest part of the lake is about 120 feet, and the surface water temperature is 58 degrees Fahrenheit. The shoreline of the lake within three to five li is sandy, and beyond that is alluvial mud.

Songjiang 86

Reinstatement of Quota at the Prosecutor's Office

This county's court, after Hu Yi-gu was assigned by the High Court to inspect Songjiang this year in January, deemed that the number of cases was low, which necessitated downsizing. A request to dismiss one prosecutor and one judge was filed. The request was then approved by the Ministry of Judicial Administration, and the prosecutor was dismissed. The duties were handled by the chief prosecutor. Prosecutor Mengzhou was reassigned elsewhere. However, the scarcity of lawsuits in January was not a reliable indicator. Recently, the number of lawsuits has increased daily, making it difficult for one person to handle them all. The court president Wang Sixian was consulted and a joint request was made to the Ministry of Judicial Administration regarding the increased number of lawsuits and reinstatement of the quota. A directive approving the request has arrived in Songjiang, and it is learned that one prosecutor will be added and will arrive in Songjiang next month.

Nanhui 87

Farmer Killed for Repaying Debt

Lu A-mei, a farmer from Xiaole Township in the Eighth District, borrowed 80 yuan from Zhu Lao-han of Tangjiaozui, Waishipile, last year. Because Zhu urgently demanded repayment, Lu sold the harvested cotton and managed to raise 75 yuan. On the day before yesterday, Lu went to Zhu's place to repay the debt. However, Zhu was not at home, so Lu took the money back. While passing through Tangjiaozui, Lu met a friend, Huang Nan, who invited Lu to Shen Zhiqing's house to smoke opium. Afterwards, they each returned home. However, the next day, a male corpse was discovered in the reeds of Ciren Township. It appeared to be a murder. Some recognized the corpse as Lu A-mei and informed Lu's family, who reported it to the Eighth District Office, which in turn reported it to the county government. Yesterday, officials were dispatched to conduct an autopsy. The autopsy revealed that the corpse had more than ten stab wounds on the head, eyes, chest, and abdomen. The suspects, Shen Zhiqing, Huang Nan, and Shen Gong, who were apprehended, are being interrogated rigorously.

Suzhou 88

Diphtheria Prevalent in Suzhou

The recent hot weather in Suzhou has led to the prevalence of diphtheria. Many patients are concentrated in the Shantang area, especially children. Cuiying Middle School in Sanliuwang has also experienced similar cases, so it has announced a six-day suspension of classes to prevent the spread of the disease.

Haimen 89

Zheng Ge on Hunger Strike in Jail

Zheng Ge, a former prison guard in this county, falsely used the name of the Nantong District Commissioner's Office to swindle and deceive others. After Commissioner Zheng learned of this, he ordered the county to arrest Zheng, who is temporarily detained in the county public security bureau's detention center. Zheng is said to be suffering from severe psychological distress, is experiencing erratic behavior, is crying and laughing uncontrollably, and is not eating. Zheng has been on a hunger strike for six days, and his condition is deteriorating daily, raising concerns about his life. Yesterday (the 27th), the county public security bureau submitted a report to the county government requesting instructions. County Magistrate Zhang instructed the bureau to send Zheng to the Tongshan Hospital for diagnosis and treatment.

Dismissal and Supervision of the Chief of the Third Sub-Bureau 90

Huang Mingsheng, the chief of the third sub-bureau of the public security bureau in Sanyang Town, the fourth district, and patrol leader Chen Gongyu, among others, were accused by Gong Fang and others of collecting donations from gambling and opium dens. County Magistrate Zhang ordered the county public security bureau to arrest Huang Mingsheng and patrol leaders Chen Gongyu, Lu Kaishan, and patrolman Lin Xuehai and send them to the county. After interrogation by Chen, Huang Mingsheng was released on bail, while Chen, Lu, and Lin were detained. County Magistrate Zhang believes that the sub-bureau chief's collection of irregular fees has been confirmed by the confessions of Chen, Lu, and Lin, and yesterday ordered the county public security bureau to dismiss Huang Mingsheng and place him under supervision to facilitate interrogation. The vacancy will be filled by Zhou Mingyi, who will be appointed as acting chief by the county public security bureau.

Wuxi 91

Unresolved Dispute Over Tobacco and Alcohol Tax

This county's tobacco and alcohol license tax collection office ordered a doubling of the tobacco and alcohol license tax rates for the current session of businesses, including liquor and sauce, sauce shops, tobacco exchange, cigarette, and native tobacco businesses, which has caused a backlash. The situation was previously reported in this newspaper. It is learned that the five trade associations have received reports from members that recently, a large number of tax office employees have been dispatched to various tobacco and liquor stores in the city and countryside, forcibly demanding double tax payments, and even taking away cigarettes and other goods from the stores without authorization, causing considerable disturbance. Upon receiving the reports, the associations convened a joint meeting again yesterday, resolving to firmly resist the tax increase. They also sent a letter to the county chamber of commerce requesting assistance to stop the tax office from harassing the market.

Robbery of Pig Boat in Taihu Lake 92

Wu Yingshan, a villager from Zoujia Alley in Zhouxin Town, Third District, has been engaged in the pig trade. Recently, Wu shipped dozens of large pigs from the Jiangbei area, intending to transport them to Hangzhou and other places in Zhejiang Province for sale. Unexpectedly, when sailing in Taihu Lake the night before last, they suddenly encountered a pirate ship. Five bandits jumped onto the pig boat and searched and robbed it for about half an hour before fleeing with their stolen goods. The incident has not yet been reported to the authorities for investigation. In addition, Liu Fengsheng from Funing came to Wuxi the day before yesterday to look for his son. Around midnight, Liu took a pedicab from Chong'an Temple to the railway station. The pedicab driver, Zeng Huirong, seeing Liu's wealth, harbored evil intentions and colluded with another pedicab driver named Chong Youfu, instructing him to wait in the deserted Houqi Street Dawang Temple. He then took a detour with Liu to that location, intending to rob him. Liu shouted for help, and Wang Dexue, a police officer from the nearby Fifth Precinct Police Station, heard the cries and went to assist Liu Fengsheng in apprehending the two pedicab drivers. They were taken to the station for interrogation.

Changzhou 93

General Situation of the Drought in Wujin This Year: The drought in Wujin this year is unprecedented in sixty years. The extent of the disaster area is also the largest seen in sixty years. In total, the disaster-stricken area in Wujin covers 813,494 mu (a Chinese unit of area, approximately 0.165 acres). Even when calculating only the severely affected areas (60% or more crop failure), there are still 673,372 mu. The disaster area spans all townships, with the most severely affected being the old Qin, Mingfeng, Jingxiao, Shangyi, Dayou, Tongjiang, Huainan, Huaibei, Anshang, Huihua, Taiping, and Dingdong townships. The preliminary survey has been completed. A table listing the affected townships and their areas is presented below:

First District: None Second District: Eighteen Tu (a local administrative unit)

Third District: Twenty-one Townships Fourth District: Thirty Tu

Fifth District: Thirty Tu Sixth District: Seventeen Townships

Seventh District: Fifteen Townships Eighth District: Thirty-six Tu

Ninth District: Seventeen Tu Tenth District: Twenty-eight Tu

Eleventh District: Nine Townships Twelfth District: Twenty-four Tu

Thirteenth District: Twenty-seven Townships Fourteenth District: Nine Townships

Fifteenth District: Fifteen Townships Sixteenth District: Twenty-three Townships

Seventeenth District: Sixteen Townships Eighteenth District: Seven Townships

Nineteenth District: Fifteen Townships

District Chief Being Watched for Allowing Robbers to Escape 94

The home of Duan Baoren, a resident of Panjiaqiao Town, Eighth District of Wuyi County, was robbed on the night of the 21st of this month. Duan's wife was also shot by the robbers. Subsequently, the Zoumatang Security Corps apprehended two key suspects in the case, Yang Jinchuan and Tang Shenggeng, on the 25th, and recovered a stolen private seal belonging to Duan Baoren. They were taken to the district office. After a preliminary interrogation by District Chief Wang Qingtong, he ordered them to be shackled and guarded by security corps members, intending to hand them over to the county for interrogation the next day. However, the robbers escaped in the middle of the night, breaking their shackles and opening the door lock. The county government, based on reports from Wu Cai and others, the heads of the Zoumatang Security Corps, accusing District Chief Wang of accepting bribes and releasing the suspects, summoned the security corps members who had been guarding the robbers on the 29th. After questioning them, the county government ordered District Chief Wang Qingtong and the two security corps members to be placed under watch. The county government ordered the assistant, Sun Shizheng, to temporarily take charge of district affairs.

Jiangyin 95

Telegram Requesting Postponement of Land Tax Collection

The county government has announced that the first installment of this year's land tax, accounting for 40%, will be collected starting on October 1st, with collection points set up in various rural areas. Now, citizens Chen Xingjie and others have telegraphed the provincial government, requesting a temporary postponement of the tax collection. A request to postpone the first installment of this year's land tax is under review. However, County Magistrate Bao Gang, despite being mindful of the people's difficulties, has decided to collect the tax starting on the first of next month. We, the common people, have long been in dire straits. We are barely able to pay the regular tax, let alone the various surcharges that have not been reduced at all. Therefore, we earnestly request Your Excellency to instruct the county government via telegram to temporarily suspend the tax collection.

Special Item

A Record of Investigation into the Jingdezhen Porcelain Industry (Part 2) by Du Chongyuan 96

There are more than a hundred porcelain kilns in Jingdezhen, all owned by a few wealthy households in Duchang. The kiln system involves calculating firewood costs based on the number of porcelain pieces. (Jingdezhen uses wood-fired kilns.) The firewood costs must be paid in advance. The kiln owners are not responsible for the quality of the firing. Moreover, the kiln owners do not need to be stationed in the town permanently; they only assign a few kiln workers to manage the affairs. The kiln workers not only do not earn salaries from the kiln owners but also have to pay them a considerable "activity fee." As for how the kiln workers make up for their losses, when the blank (unfired porcelain) producers fire their pieces, they have to pay the kiln workers a commission (commonly known as "rou jin," literally "meat money," which is simply a bribe). If the blank producers do not pay the "rou jin," the kiln workers can arbitrarily damage the blanks or place them in areas with low or high firing temperatures, making them susceptible to kiln collapses. Therefore, the blank producers have no choice but to pay the commission. Recently, due to the sluggish business environment, kiln owners, in order to seek greater profits, arbitrarily enlarged the kiln bodies to accommodate more porcelain pieces and collect more firewood money. However, with larger kiln bodies, the firing temperature is bound to be higher. When the firing temperature is high, the saggars (protective ceramic boxes) cannot withstand it, and kiln collapses are becoming more frequent. The kiln owners do not care. Even worse, the kiln owners implement kiln restrictions to increase firewood money. What are kiln restrictions? They mean that the kiln owners collude to limit the firing frequency. Kilns that can be fired eight times a month are restricted to only two or three times. In this way, the blank producers cannot wait and have to let the kiln owners dictate the price, even if it is high. As a result, the blank producers suffer more losses, and their costs increase. Higher costs lead to slow sales, and fewer people engage in blank production. With fewer people making blanks, the kiln owners and saggar factories exert even more pressure. The outcome is mutual destruction. However, this is only the internal injury. As for the external factors, such as inconvenient transportation, frequent conflicts with bandits, and the global economic depression that has swept into Jingdezhen, the future seems even bleaker. In recent years, the number of kiln owners (blank producers) has decreased from 4,000 to 1,000, and the number of workers has decreased from 100,000 to 40,000. The total business volume has shrunk from 1.45 million yuan to 2-3 million yuan. Every year-end, honest kiln owners and workers often hang themselves, while cunning ones become bandits. The roads are filthy, and the people look malnourished. In the entire town, it is impossible to find a child with rosy cheeks. The three managers from the Bank of China who accompanied me were all round-faced, stout, and portly. Mr. Zhou Xiaofang weighed 242 pounds, Mr. Cai Shenzhai weighed 219 pounds, and Mr. Zhou Daren weighed 217 pounds. When they walked through the streets, the townspeople flocked to watch, as if they were seeing strange creatures. This shows that the town had never seen such blessed people with round faces and big bellies. The town is known for its "five excesses": opium, prostitutes, bedbugs, latrines, and dead rats. Therefore, plague epidemics have occurred over the years. Recently, since the special operations unit of the Nanchang Headquarters arrived in the town and implemented intervention and ordered cleanliness, the situation is better than before. The above rambling description gives a general picture of Jingdezhen.

As for rescuing Jingdezhen, it is not without solutions; it only depends on whether the government has the determination. People who have visited Jingdezhen over the years always say how each industry is controlled and how stubborn the workers are, as if the source of Jingdezhen's industry's illness lies entirely there. In reality, this is just a symptom of Jingdezhen, not the cause. What is the cause? It is the government's laissez-faire attitude. In past dynasties, Jingdezhen had kiln officials who specialized in managing these matters. They thoroughly understood the workers' hardships and labor-management disputes and could guide them accordingly. Since the Republic of China, a purely laissez-faire policy has been adopted, with local officials acting as managers. (During the Hongxian era, a pottery industry supervisor was established once for the reconstruction of the imperial kiln.) However, local officials are not familiar with the pottery industry and deal with matters perfunctorily. Dishonest individuals see it as a source of wealth. Therefore, the Jingdezhen County Magistrate and the Chief of the Public Security Bureau are known as lucrative positions. Imagine putting hundreds of thousands of ignorant people in positions with conflicting interests; disputes are inevitable. Whenever disputes arise, the government cannot resolve them, or even if they do, it is not fair. The workers can only follow ancient methods or resort to force to resolve them themselves. Adhering to ancient methods is close to stubbornness, and using force only leads to more disputes. As a result, the strong bully the weak, the majority abuse the minority, they are reckless and destructive, and the situation has become so broken and fragmented. The solution is for the government to establish a pottery administration and management agency, elevate its position, expand its authority, and choose someone who is knowledgeable about the pottery industry and passionate about workers' welfare to hold the position for a long time. They should handle matters directly without delay. The workers are inherently afraid of the government, so as long as the measures are appropriate, they will all be happy. The pottery administration and management agency should establish a raw material refining factory. All raw materials should be purchased by the government at low prices and refined mechanically, then sold to blank producers at low prices. At the same time, a model porcelain factory should be established to demonstrate porcelain manufacturing methods, the benefits of cooperation, and the conversion to coal-fired kilns to reduce costs and eliminate the evils of kiln restrictions. Then, a model cooperative should be established for cooperative purchasing and cooperative marketing. All symptoms of control can be swept away. As for fundamental solutions, it is especially necessary to improve transportation. In the past, Jingdezhen's transportation relied entirely on the Rao River, which connects to Poyang Lake. However, the upper reaches of the Rao River are shallow and have many shoals. In the autumn, the water is dry, and it often takes months to reach Hukou, which is time-consuming and causes a lot of damage, greatly affecting sales. Recently, it was reported that the Jinghu Highway (from Jingdezhen to Hukou) has been repaired. It would be better to convert the highway into a railway, laying only light rails and purchasing a small locomotive for freight transportation. Not only would it facilitate the transportation of porcelain, but it would also provide an outlet for tea from Wuyuan and Qimen. In this way, both internal and external problems can be addressed, and all ills can be eliminated. Not only will the original state be restored, but it will also be promoted and expanded. Recent progress has been made in Jingdezhen's artistic products, but unfortunately, there is no one to connect them for cooperation, encouragement, and learning from each other, resulting in unscrupulous merchants making one bottle in the east and painting one color in the west, earning hundreds of times the profit through repeated labor. Therefore, although many porcelain makers in Jingdezhen have been losing money in recent years, porcelain vendors everywhere have been making fortunes. (These porcelain vendors refer specifically to those dealing in artistic goods, not ordinary porcelain merchants.) This is all due to the ignorance of the workers, who do not know how to cooperate. All of these things should be changed and reorganized by the pottery administration and management agency through organization and training. When Jingdezhen's porcelain industry has improved slightly and the workers' lives have gradually stabilized, then further research on worker education and public health should be conducted. Only then will Jingdezhen have a promising future.

The estimated costs for rescuing the Jingdezhen porcelain industry are as follows:

Raw material refining factory: 100,000 yuan

Model porcelain factory: 200,000 yuan

Various cooperatives: 150,000 yuan

Education subsidies and research expenses: 50,000 yuan

Annual operating expenses for the pottery administration and management agency: 20,000 yuan

Light rail and locomotives (280 li [approximately 93 miles]): Separate budget to be determined by experts (End)

Ping An Company's Baohua Steamer

Detained by Qidong County 103

Due to Lawsuit Filed by Families of Those Who Drowned After the Ship Ran Aground

Shipping Trade Association Cables Requesting Release

New Voice News Agency reports: The Shanghai-to-Sha Line Baohua steamer of the Ping An Commercial Shipping Company sailed from Shanghai to Sha on the 27th of this month. On the 28th, after arriving at Antou Port, it was detained by the Qidong County government. The captain was arrested. The reason is that the families of the passengers who drowned on the 12th of this month after the ship ran aground at Sanhe Port filed a lawsuit. The details are as follows:

Crew Members Detained 104

Ren Rugui, a worker, and Liu Zhichang, a tea server, who drowned after the Baohua steamer ran aground at Sanhe Port on the 12th of this month, have been recovered and buried. The company has provided compensation. The steamer sailed from Shanghai to Sha at 5:00 PM on the 27th of this month. On the 28th, after arriving at Antou Port at 10:00 AM, the Qidong County government sent armed police to detain the steamer and assigned police to guard the ship. At the same time, the shipowner and crew members were arrested and taken to the county government. The reason is that the families of the drowned passengers filed a lawsuit with the county government.

Shipowner Telegraphs 105

The captain of the Baohua steamer immediately telegraphed the Ping An General Company in Shanghai to report the detention. The company immediately telegraphed its office at Antou Port to inquire about the details of the detention. It then received a reply telegram stating, "It is known that the detention of the Baohua steamer is due to a lawsuit. The captain has been interrogated and detained. Send a person in charge to come quickly and ask someone influential to handle the matter." The company immediately reported to the Shanghai Shipping Trade Association, requesting that it telegraph the county to release the ship in order to facilitate transportation. At the same time, it also reported to the Shanghai Shipping Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation.

Requesting Release by Telegram 106

The Shipping Trade Association telegraphed Qidong County:

To County Magistrate Li of the Qidong County Government: According to a report from member Ping An Company, we received a telegram from the Antou Port Bureau stating that the Baohua steamer has been detained and all staff members have been taken to the county government, etc. We do not know the reason and are deeply shocked. If it is due to the previous grounding of our ship at Sanhe Port, then our ship has properly handled the aftermath of the accident for the crew and passengers, and whether the crew members were at fault has also been reported to the Shanghai Shipping Administration Bureau, the competent authority, for thorough investigation and assessment. The company's ships are all registered and licensed, so even if someone files a lawsuit, there is no risk of escape. Ships are related to transportation, and the company is responsible for responding to the lawsuit, so there is no need to detain the ship. Please have the public association telegram the county government to release our ship and allow the crew members to be released on bail. If there is a lawsuit, our company will be responsible for responding to it, so as to avoid losses and maintain transportation. This is a matter of public interest, and we hope for a reply by telegram. Yu Kouyan, Standing Committee Member of the Shanghai Shipping Association.

Impact on Transportation 107

The ships operating on the Shanghai-to-Sha line, on odd days, are the Ping An Company's Baohua steamer, the Yuxing Company's Xinrenhe steamer, and the Daxing Company's Fuxing steamer. On even days, they are the Zaida Company's Guangxiang steamer and the Jufeng Company's Baofeng steamer, for a total of five ships. Since the Baohua steamer, which operates on odd days, was detained, and the Xinrenhe steamer is currently undergoing repairs, only the Fuxing steamer is operating. The Fuxing steamer has a net tonnage of 372 tons and limited passenger capacity. The number of passengers traveling from Shanghai to Sha or from Sha to Shanghai every day is quite large, so the Fuxing steamer cannot load them all, which has an impact on transportation.

Shipping Administration Bureau Telegram 108

After receiving a report from the Ping An Company, the Shanghai Shipping Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation telegraphed the Qidong County government, "According to a report from the Ping An Commercial Shipping Company, the Baohua steamer has been detained. What is the reason? Please reply by telegram." A New Voice News Agency reporter interviewed Li Yaoting, the manager of the Ping An Company, at the Atlantic Western Restaurant last night. According to him, in the case of the Baohua steamer running aground at Sanhe Port, the company has provided generous compensation to the families of the drowned worker and tea server, and there were no drowned passengers. It is deeply shocking that County Magistrate Li of Qidong County detained the ship. The Shipping Trade Association, etc., have telegraphed the county to release the ship, but as of this moment, no reply telegram has been received from the county. The Ministry of Transportation Sends Personnel to the UK

To Expand Direct Sino-British Telegraph Services 109

Yu Senwen Arrives in Shanghai from Nanjing Yesterday to Prepare for Departure

Ordered to Concurrently Investigate Vocational Education in Europe

Shenshi News Agency reports: The Ministry of Transportation believes that Sino-British telecommunications are very important after the international radio station began direct Sino-British communications. Therefore, the transportation authorities attach great importance to this. Since the line was implemented in May of this year, there has been a need to actively plan for the development and expansion of telecommunications. Recently, Yu Senwen, the chairman of the Employee Affairs Committee of the Ministry, was specially sent to the UK to serve as the Ministry's resident commissioner in the UK's International Telecommunications Bureau, responsible for contacting and promoting this initiative. Yu arrived in Shanghai yesterday and visited Wen Yuqing, the director of the International Telecommunications Bureau, to discuss the measures to be taken to contact the British side. Yu has now decided to take the Italian postal ship Conte Verde to the UK in the next few days.

Expanding Sino-British Telecommunications 110

According to Yu yesterday, his mission to the UK is to discuss and plan with the British side on matters related to direct Sino-British radio communications. Because of the agreement made between the two sides at the beginning of the direct communication business between China and the UK in May of this year, it stated that there should be a balance of telegrams between the two countries in order to achieve the principle of equality in telegraph fee revenue. Since the opening of communications, according to statistics, the average number of telegrams sent from our country per day is about seventy or eighty, while the average number of telegrams from the UK is only about twenty, accounting for only one-quarter, which puts our side at a considerable disadvantage. The reason for the imbalance is that in addition to the direct line of Sino-British cooperation for wireless telecommunications between the UK and our country, the UK also has the Sannorth Wireless Telegraph Company, which can send telegrams to the Far East. The British people are accustomed to sending telegrams to the Sannorth Company, so the direct Sino-British line has been affected. Even the overseas Chinese in the UK are mostly not fully aware of the significance of direct Sino-British communications and have not fully utilized the line. Therefore, Yu's mission to the UK is to contact the British side and, at the same time, plan and promote publicity in the UK to develop Sino-British telecommunications.

Investigating Vocational Education 111

In addition to handling Sino-British telecommunications, Yu has also been specially assigned by the Ministry to investigate the implementation of vocational education in various advanced industrial countries in Europe, such as Germany, France, Italy, the UK, and Switzerland, after completing his work in the UK. He will also pay attention to labor management, employee administration, and other aspects to serve as a reference for our country's improvement. Yu, who was the chairman of the Employee Affairs Committee of the Ministry of Transportation, has made considerable achievements in the past in the education and management of transportation employees in our country. It is believed that his return from this overseas investigation will bring a new contribution. It is reported that Yu's trip is scheduled for one year.
